***utopie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:utopie.html>utopie</a> (62564)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:New Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:new.html>New</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">Ūtopia</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:utopie.html>utopie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:utopie.html>utopieën</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:utopie.html>utopietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:utopia.html>Utopia</a>, imaginary <a href = vnd.unilang:society.html>society</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:perfect.html>perfect</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:harmony.html>harmony</a></li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:utopia.html>utopia</a>, unattainable <a href = vnd.unilang:ideal.html>ideal</a></li>

***uurwerk.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uurwerk.html>uurwerk</a> (24012)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">urewerc</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>Equivalent</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uur.html>uur</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:werk.html>werk</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uurwerk.html>uurwerk</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uurwerken.html>uurwerken</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uurwerk.html>uurwerkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>timekeeping mechanism, <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:device.html>device</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:such.html>such</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> mechanism, <a href = vnd.unilang:such.html>such</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:as.html>as</a>:
